"main.py
```python
'''
This file contains the main GUI application that interacts with other components.
'''
import tkinter as tk
from google_ads_api_handler import GoogleAdsAPIHandler
class GoogleAdsConverterApp:
    def __init__(self, master):
        self.master = master
        self.master.title("Google Ads Converter App")
        self.api_handler = GoogleAdsAPIHandler(client_id='your_client_id', client_secret='your_client_secret', developer_token='your_developer_token', refresh_token='your_refresh_token')
        self.initialize_gui()
    def initialize_gui(self):
        # GUI initialization code goes here
        upload_button = tk.Button(self.master, text="Upload Conversions", command=self.upload_conversions)
        upload_button.pack()
    def upload_conversions(self):
        file_path = 'path_to_your_csv_file.csv'
        conversion_data = self.api_handler.read_csv_file(file_path)
        if conversion_data:
            self.api_handler.authenticate()  # Explicitly call authenticate
            self.api_handler.upload_conversions(conversion_data)
            print("Conversions uploaded successfully!")
        else:
            print("Error reading CSV file.")
def main():
    root = tk.Tk()
    app = GoogleAdsConverterApp(root)
    root.mainloop()
if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()
```

google_ads_api_handler.py
```python
'''
This file contains the Google Ads API handler class.
'''
from google.ads.google_ads.client import GoogleAdsClient
from google.ads.google_ads.errors import GoogleAdsException
from google.ads.google_ads.v8.services import conversion_action_service_pb2
from google.ads.google_ads.v8.services import conversion_upload_service_pb2
from google.protobuf import field_mask_pb2
class GoogleAdsAPIHandler:
    def __init__(self, client_id, client_secret, developer_token, refresh_token):
        self.client_id = client_id
        self.client_secret = client_secret
        self.developer_token = developer_token
        self.refresh_token = refresh_token
        self.client = None  # Initialize client as None
    def authenticate(self):
        try:
            self.client = GoogleAdsClient.load_from_storage()
        except FileNotFoundError:
            self.client = GoogleAdsClient(
                load_from_storage=False,
                developer_token=self.developer_token,
                refresh_token=self.refresh_token,
                client_id=self.client_id,
                client_secret=self.client_secret
            )
            self.client.refresh_access_token()
    def read_csv_file(self, file_path):
        conversion_data = []
        try:
            with open(file_path, 'r') as file:
                for line in file:
                    data = line.strip().split(',')
                    if len(data) == 4:
                        conversion_data.append({
                            'gclid': data[0],
                            'gbraid': data[1],
                            'wbraid': data[2],
                            'conversion_value': float(data[3])
                        })
        except FileNotFoundError:
            print("Error: File not found.")
        except Exception as e:
            print(f"Error reading CSV file: {e}")
        return conversion_data
    def upload_conversions(self, conversion_data):
        try:
            conversion_action_resource_name = 'INSERT_YOUR_CONVERSION_ACTION_RESOURCE_NAME_HERE'
            conversion_upload_service = self.client.get_service('ConversionUploadService')
            for conversion in conversion_data:
                upload_conversion = conversion_upload_service_pb2.UploadCallConversionRequest()
                upload_conversion.conversion_action = conversion_action_resource_name
                upload_conversion.conversion_value = conversion['conversion_value']
                upload_conversion.call_duration_seconds = 120  # Example call duration
                if 'gclid' in conversion:
                    upload_conversion.gclid = conversion['gclid']
                elif 'gbraid' in conversion:
                    upload_conversion.order_id = conversion['gbraid']
                elif 'wbraid' in conversion:
                    upload_conversion.order_id = conversion['wbraid']
                response = conversion_upload_service.upload_call_conversions(
                    customer_id=self.client.customer_id,
                    requests=[upload_conversion]
                )
                print(f"Uploaded conversion for {upload_conversion.gclid or upload_conversion.order_id} successfully.")
        except GoogleAdsException as ex:
            print(f'Request with ID "{ex.request_id}" failed with status "{ex.error.code().name}" and includes the following errors:')
            for error in ex.failure.errors:
                print(f'\tError with message "{error.message}".')
        except Exception as e:
            print(f"An error occurred while uploading conversions: {e}")
```

```python
'''
This file contains the Google Ads API handler class.
'''
# Ensure that the Google Ads API client library is installed:
# You can install it using pip:
# pip install google-ads

from google.ads.google_ads.client import GoogleAdsClient
from google.ads.google_ads.errors import GoogleAdsException
from google.ads.google_ads.v8.services import conversion_action_service_pb2
from google.ads.google_ads.v8.services import conversion_upload_service_pb2
from google.protobuf import field_mask_pb2

class GoogleAdsAPIHandler:
    def __init__(self, client_id, client_secret, developer_token, refresh_token):
        self.client_id = client_id
        self.client_secret = client_secret
        self.developer_token = developer_token
        self.refresh_token = refresh_token
        self.client = None  # Initialize client as None
    
    def authenticate(self):
        try:
            self.client = GoogleAdsClient.load_from_storage()
        except FileNotFoundError:
            self.client = GoogleAdsClient(
                load_from_storage=False,
                developer_token=self.developer_token,
                refresh_token=self.refresh_token,
                client_id=self.client_id,
                client_secret=self.client_secret
            )
            self.client.refresh_access_token()
    
    def read_csv_file(self, file_path):
        conversion_data = []
        try:
            with open(file_path, 'r') as file:
                for line in file:
                    data = line.strip().split(',')
                    if len(data) == 4:
                        conversion_data.append({
                            'gclid': data[0],
                            'gbraid': data[1],
                            'wbraid': data[2],
                            'conversion_value': float(data[3])
                        })
        except FileNotFoundError:
            print("Error: File not found.")
        except Exception as e:
            print(f"Error reading CSV file: {e}")
        return conversion_data
    
    def upload_conversions(self, conversion_data):
        try:
            conversion_action_resource_name = 'INSERT_YOUR_CONVERSION_ACTION_RESOURCE_NAME_HERE'
            conversion_upload_service = self.client.get_service('ConversionUploadService')
            for conversion in conversion_data:
                upload_conversion = conversion_upload_service_pb2.UploadCallConversionRequest()
                upload_conversion.conversion_action = conversion_action_resource_name
                upload_conversion.conversion_value = conversion['conversion_value']
                upload_conversion.call_duration_seconds = 120  # Example call duration
                if 'gclid' in conversion:
                    upload_conversion.gclid = conversion['gclid']
                elif 'gbraid' in conversion:
                    upload_conversion.order_id = conversion['gbraid']
                elif 'wbraid' in conversion:
                    upload_conversion.order_id = conversion['wbraid']
                response = conversion_upload_service.upload_call_conversions(
                    customer_id=self.client.customer_id,
                    requests=[upload_conversion]
                )
                print(f"Uploaded conversion for {upload_conversion.gclid or upload_conversion.order_id} successfully.")
        except GoogleAdsException as ex:
            print(f'Request with ID "{ex.request_id}" failed with status "{ex.error.code().name}" and includes the following errors:')
            for error in ex.failure.errors:
                print(f'\tError with message "{error.message}".')
        except Exception as e:
            print(f"An error occurred while uploading conversions: {e}")

'''
This file contains the Google Ads API handler class.
'''
# Ensure that the Google Ads API client library is installed:
# You can install it using pip:
# pip install google-ads

from google.ads.google_ads.client import GoogleAdsClient
from google.ads.google_ads.errors import GoogleAdsException
from google.ads.google_ads.v8.services import conversion_action_service_pb2
from google.ads.google_ads.v8.services import conversion_upload_service_pb2
from google.protobuf import field_mask_pb2

class GoogleAdsAPIHandler:
    def __init__(self, client_id, client_secret, developer_token, refresh_token):
        self.client_id = client_id
        self.client_secret = client_secret
        self.developer_token = developer_token
        self.refresh_token = refresh_token
        self.client = None  # Initialize client as None
    
    def authenticate(self):
        try:
            self.client = GoogleAdsClient.load_from_storage()
        except FileNotFoundError:
            self.client = GoogleAdsClient(
                load_from_storage=False,
                developer_token=self.developer_token,
                refresh_token=self.refresh_token,
                client_id=self.client_id,
                client_secret=self.client_secret
            )
            self.client.refresh_access_token()
    
    def read_csv_file(self, file_path):
        conversion_data = []
        try:
            with open(file_path, 'r') as file:
                for line in file:
                    data = line.strip().split(',')
                    if len(data) == 4:
                        conversion_data.append({
                            'gclid': data[0],
                            'gbraid': data[1],
                            'wbraid': data[2],
                            'conversion_value': float(data[3])
                        })
        except FileNotFoundError:
            print("Error: File not found.")
        except Exception as e:
            print(f"Error reading CSV file: {e}")
        return conversion_data
    
    def upload_conversions(self, conversion_data):
        try:
            conversion_action_resource_name = 'INSERT_YOUR_CONVERSION_ACTION_RESOURCE_NAME_HERE'
            conversion_upload_service = self.client.get_service('ConversionUploadService')
            for conversion in conversion_data:
                upload_conversion = conversion_upload_service_pb2.UploadCallConversionRequest()
                upload_conversion.conversion_action = conversion_action_resource_name
                upload_conversion.conversion_value = conversion['conversion_value']
                upload_conversion.call_duration_seconds = 120  # Example call duration
                if 'gclid' in conversion:
                    upload_conversion.gclid = conversion['gclid']
                elif 'gbraid' in conversion:
                    upload_conversion.order_id = conversion['gbraid']
                elif 'wbraid' in conversion:
                    upload_conversion.order_id = conversion['wbraid']
                response = conversion_upload_service.upload_call_conversions(
                    customer_id=self.client.customer_id,
                    requests=[upload_conversion]
                )
                print(f"Uploaded conversion for {upload_conversion.gclid or upload_conversion.order_id} successfully.")
        except GoogleAdsException as ex:
            print(f'Request with ID "{ex.request_id}" failed with status "{ex.error.code().name}" and includes the following errors:')
            for error in ex.failure.errors:
                print(f'\tError with message "{error.message}".')
        except Exception as e:
            print(f"An error occurred while uploading conversions: {e}")

"main.py
```python
'''
This file contains the main GUI application that interacts with other components.
'''
import tkinter as tk
from google_ads_api_handler import GoogleAdsAPIHandler
class GoogleAdsConverterApp:
    def __init__(self, master):
        self.master = master
        self.master.title("Google Ads Converter App")
        self.api_handler = GoogleAdsAPIHandler(client_id='your_client_id', client_secret='your_client_secret', developer_token='your_developer_token', refresh_token='your_refresh_token')
        self.initialize_gui()
    def initialize_gui(self):
        # GUI initialization code goes here
        upload_button = tk.Button(self.master, text="Upload Conversions", command=self.upload_conversions)
        upload_button.pack()
    def upload_conversions(self):
        file_path = 'path_to_your_csv_file.csv'
        conversion_data = self.api_handler.read_csv_file(file_path)
        if conversion_data:
            self.api_handler.authenticate()  # Explicitly call authenticate
            self.api_handler.upload_conversions(conversion_data)
            print("Conversions uploaded successfully!")
        else:
            print("Error reading CSV file.")
def main():
    root = tk.Tk()
    app = GoogleAdsConverterApp(root)
    root.mainloop()
if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()
```

google_ads_api_handler.py
```python
'''
This file contains the Google Ads API handler class.
'''
from google.ads.google_ads.client import GoogleAdsClient
from google.ads.google_ads.errors import GoogleAdsException
from google.ads.google_ads.v8.services import conversion_action_service_pb2
from google.ads.google_ads.v8.services import conversion_upload_service_pb2
from google.protobuf import field_mask_pb2
class GoogleAdsAPIHandler:
    def __init__(self, client_id, client_secret, developer_token, refresh_token):
        self.client_id = client_id
        self.client_secret = client_secret
        self.developer_token = developer_token
        self.refresh_token = refresh_token
        self.client = None  # Initialize client as None
    def authenticate(self):
        try:
            self.client = GoogleAdsClient.load_from_storage()
        except FileNotFoundError:
            self.client = GoogleAdsClient(
                load_from_storage=False,
                developer_token=self.developer_token,
                refresh_token=self.refresh_token,
                client_id=self.client_id,
                client_secret=self.client_secret
            )
            self.client.refresh_access_token()
    def read_csv_file(self, file_path):
        conversion_data = []
        try:
            with open(file_path, 'r') as file:
                for line in file:
                    data = line.strip().split(',')
                    if len(data) == 4:
                        conversion_data.append({
                            'gclid': data[0],
                            'gbraid': data[1],
                            'wbraid': data[2],
                            'conversion_value': float(data[3])
                        })
        except FileNotFoundError:
            print("Error: File not found.")
        except Exception as e:
            print(f"Error reading CSV file: {e}")
        return conversion_data
    def upload_conversions(self, conversion_data):
        try:
            conversion_action_resource_name = 'INSERT_YOUR_CONVERSION_ACTION_RESOURCE_NAME_HERE'
            conversion_upload_service = self.client.get_service('ConversionUploadService')
            for conversion in conversion_data:
                upload_conversion = conversion_upload_service_pb2.UploadCallConversionRequest()
                upload_conversion.conversion_action = conversion_action_resource_name
                upload_conversion.conversion_value = conversion['conversion_value']
                upload_conversion.call_duration_seconds = 120  # Example call duration
                if 'gclid' in conversion:
                    upload_conversion.gclid = conversion['gclid']
                elif 'gbraid' in conversion:
                    upload_conversion.order_id = conversion['gbraid']
                elif 'wbraid' in conversion:
                    upload_conversion.order_id = conversion['wbraid']
                response = conversion_upload_service.upload_call_conversions(
                    customer_id=self.client.customer_id,
                    requests=[upload_conversion]
                )
                print(f"Uploaded conversion for {upload_conversion.gclid or upload_conversion.order_id} successfully.")
        except GoogleAdsException as ex:
            print(f'Request with ID "{ex.request_id}" failed with status "{ex.error.code().name}" and includes the following errors:')
            for error in ex.failure.errors:
                print(f'\tError with message "{error.message}".')
        except Exception as e:
            print(f"An error occurred while uploading conversions: {e}")
```

Task: "Please help me implement a Python program that uses the Google Ads API to read a local CSV file containing offline conversion data, uploads conversions to a specified Google Ads Conversion Action using the appropriate identifiers (GCLID, GBRAID, or WBRAID), implements OAuth2 authentication, and includes basic error handling and logging.".

"main.py
```python
'''
This file contains the main GUI application that interacts with other components.
'''
import tkinter as tk
from google_ads_api_handler import GoogleAdsAPIHandler
class GoogleAdsConverterApp:
    def __init__(self, master):
        self.master = master
        self.master.title("Google Ads Converter App")
        self.api_handler = GoogleAdsAPIHandler(client_id='your_client_id', client_secret='your_client_secret', developer_token='your_developer_token', refresh_token='your_refresh_token')
        self.initialize_gui()
    def initialize_gui(self):
        # GUI initialization code goes here
        upload_button = tk.Button(self.master, text="Upload Conversions", command=self.upload_conversions)
        upload_button.pack()
    def upload_conversions(self):
        file_path = 'path_to_your_csv_file.csv'
        conversion_data = self.api_handler.read_csv_file(file_path)
        if conversion_data:
            self.api_handler.authenticate()  # Explicitly call authenticate
            self.api_handler.upload_conversions(conversion_data)
            print("Conversions uploaded successfully!")
        else:
            print("Error reading CSV file.")
def main():
    root = tk.Tk()
    app = GoogleAdsConverterApp(root)
    root.mainloop()
if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()
```

google_ads_api_handler.py
```python
'''
This file contains the Google Ads API handler class.
'''
from google.ads.google_ads.client import GoogleAdsClient
from google.ads.google_ads.errors import GoogleAdsException
from google.ads.google_ads.v8.services import conversion_action_service_pb2
from google.ads.google_ads.v8.services import conversion_upload_service_pb2
from google.protobuf import field_mask_pb2
class GoogleAdsAPIHandler:
    def __init__(self, client_id, client_secret, developer_token, refresh_token):
        self.client_id = client_id
        self.client_secret = client_secret
        self.developer_token = developer_token
        self.refresh_token = refresh_token
        self.client = None  # Initialize client as None
    def authenticate(self):
        try:
            self.client = GoogleAdsClient.load_from_storage()
        except FileNotFoundError:
            self.client = GoogleAdsClient(
                load_from_storage=False,
                developer_token=self.developer_token,
                refresh_token=self.refresh_token,
                client_id=self.client_id,
                client_secret=self.client_secret
            )
            self.client.refresh_access_token()
    def read_csv_file(self, file_path):
        conversion_data = []
        try:
            with open(file_path, 'r') as file:
                for line in file:
                    data = line.strip().split(',')
                    if len(data) == 4:
                        conversion_data.append({
                            'gclid': data[0],
                            'gbraid': data[1],
                            'wbraid': data[2],
                            'conversion_value': float(data[3])
                        })
        except FileNotFoundError:
            print("Error: File not found.")
        except Exception as e:
            print(f"Error reading CSV file: {e}")
        return conversion_data
    def upload_conversions(self, conversion_data):
        try:
            conversion_action_resource_name = 'INSERT_YOUR_CONVERSION_ACTION_RESOURCE_NAME_HERE'
            conversion_upload_service = self.client.get_service('ConversionUploadService')
            for conversion in conversion_data:
                upload_conversion = conversion_upload_service_pb2.UploadCallConversionRequest()
                upload_conversion.conversion_action = conversion_action_resource_name
                upload_conversion.conversion_value = conversion['conversion_value']
                upload_conversion.call_duration_seconds = 120  # Example call duration
                if 'gclid' in conversion:
                    upload_conversion.gclid = conversion['gclid']
                elif 'gbraid' in conversion:
                    upload_conversion.order_id = conversion['gbraid']
                elif 'wbraid' in conversion:
                    upload_conversion.order_id = conversion['wbraid']
                response = conversion_upload_service.upload_call_conversions(
                    customer_id=self.client.customer_id,
                    requests=[upload_conversion]
                )
                print(f"Uploaded conversion for {upload_conversion.gclid or upload_conversion.order_id} successfully.")
        except GoogleAdsException as ex:
            print(f'Request with ID "{ex.request_id}" failed with status "{ex.error.code().name}" and includes the following errors:')
            for error in ex.failure.errors:
                print(f'\tError with message "{error.message}".')
        except Exception as e:
            print(f"An error occurred while uploading conversions: {e}")
```

"main.py
```python
'''
This file contains the main GUI application that interacts with other components.
'''
import tkinter as tk
from google_ads_api_handler import GoogleAdsAPIHandler
class GoogleAdsConverterApp:
    def __init__(self, master):
        self.master = master
        self.master.title("Google Ads Converter App")
        self.api_handler = GoogleAdsAPIHandler(client_id='your_client_id', client_secret='your_client_secret', developer_token='your_developer_token', refresh_token='your_refresh_token')
        self.initialize_gui()
    def initialize_gui(self):
        # GUI initialization code goes here
        upload_button = tk.Button(self.master, text="Upload Conversions", command=self.upload_conversions)
        upload_button.pack()
    def upload_conversions(self):
        file_path = 'path_to_your_csv_file.csv'
        conversion_data = self.api_handler.read_csv_file(file_path)
        if conversion_data:
            self.api_handler.authenticate()  # Explicitly call authenticate
            self.api_handler.upload_conversions(conversion_data)
            print("Conversions uploaded successfully!")
        else:
            print("Error reading CSV file.")
def main():
    root = tk.Tk()
    app = GoogleAdsConverterApp(root)
    root.mainloop()
if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()

google_ads_api_handler.py
```python
'''
This file contains the Google Ads API handler class.
'''
from google.ads.google_ads.client import GoogleAdsClient
from google.ads.google_ads.errors import GoogleAdsException
from google.ads.google_ads.v8.services import conversion_action_service_pb2
from google.ads.google_ads.v8.services import conversion_upload_service_pb2
from google.protobuf import field_mask_pb2
class GoogleAdsAPIHandler:
    def __init__(self, client_id, client_secret, developer_token, refresh_token):
        self.client_id = client_id
        self.client_secret = client_secret
        self.developer_token = developer_token
        self.refresh_token = refresh_token
        self.client = None  # Initialize client as None
    def authenticate(self):
        try:
            self.client = GoogleAdsClient.load_from_storage()
        except FileNotFoundError:
            self.client = GoogleAdsClient(
                load_from_storage=False,
                developer_token=self.developer_token,
                refresh_token=self.refresh_token,
                client_id=self.client_id,
                client_secret=self.client_secret
            )
            self.client.refresh_access_token()
    def read_csv_file(self, file_path):
        conversion_data = []
        try:
            with open(file_path, 'r') as file:
                for line in file:
                    data = line.strip().split(',')
                    if len(data) == 4:
                        conversion_data.append({
                            'gclid': data[0],
                            'gbraid': data[1],
                            'wbraid': data[2],
                            'conversion_value': float(data[3])
                        })
        except FileNotFoundError:
            print("Error: File not found.")
        except Exception as e:
            print(f"Error reading CSV file: {e}")
        return conversion_data
    def upload_conversions(self, conversion_data):
        try:
            conversion_action_resource_name = 'INSERT_YOUR_CONVERSION_ACTION_RESOURCE_NAME_HERE'
            conversion_upload_service = self.client.get_service('ConversionUploadService')
            for conversion in conversion_data:
                upload_conversion = conversion_upload_service_pb2.UploadCallConversionRequest()
                upload_conversion.conversion_action = conversion_action_resource_name
                upload_conversion.conversion_value = conversion['conversion_value']
                upload_conversion.call_duration_seconds = 120  # Example call duration
                if 'gclid' in conversion:
                    upload_conversion.gclid = conversion['gclid']
                elif 'gbraid' in conversion:
                    upload_conversion.order_id = conversion['gbraid']
                elif 'wbraid' in conversion:
                    upload_conversion.order_id = conversion['wbraid']
                response = conversion_upload_service.upload_call_conversions(
                    customer_id=self.client.customer_id,
                    requests=[upload_conversion]
                )
                print(f"Uploaded conversion for {upload_conversion.gclid or upload_conversion.order_id} successfully.")
        except GoogleAdsException as ex:
            print(f'Request with ID "{ex.request_id}" failed with status "{ex.error.code().name}" and includes the following errors:')
            for error in ex.failure.errors:
                print(f'\tError with message "{error.message}".')
        except Exception as e:
            print(f"An error occurred while uploading conversions: {e}")
```

google_ads_api_handler.py
```python
'''
This file contains the Google Ads API handler class.
'''
from google.ads.google_ads.client import GoogleAdsClient
from google.ads.google_ads.errors import GoogleAdsException
from google.ads.google_ads.v8.services import conversion_action_service_pb2
from google.ads.google_ads.v8.services import conversion_upload_service_pb2
from google.protobuf import field_mask_pb2
class GoogleAdsAPIHandler:
    def __init__(self, client_id, client_secret, developer_token, refresh_token):
        self.client_id = client_id
        self.client_secret = client_secret
        self.developer_token = developer_token
        self.refresh_token = refresh_token
        self.client = None  # Initialize client as None
    def authenticate(self):
        try:
            self.client = GoogleAdsClient.load_from_storage()
        except FileNotFoundError:
            self.client = GoogleAdsClient(
                load_from_storage=False,
                developer_token=self.developer_token,
                refresh_token=self.refresh_token,
                client_id=self.client_id,
                client_secret=self.client_secret
            )
            self.client.refresh_access_token()
    def read_csv_file(self, file_path):
        conversion_data = []
        try:
            with open(file_path, 'r') as file:
                for line in file:
                    data = line.strip().split(',')
                    if len(data) == 4:
                        conversion_data.append({
                            'gclid': data[0],
                            'gbraid': data[1],
                            'wbraid': data[2],
                            'conversion_value': float(data[3])
                        })
        except FileNotFoundError:
            print("Error: File not found.")
        except Exception as e:
            print(f"Error reading CSV file: {e}")
        return conversion_data
    def upload_conversions(self, conversion_data):
        try:
            conversion_action_resource_name = 'INSERT_YOUR_CONVERSION_ACTION_RESOURCE_NAME_HERE'
            conversion_upload_service = self.client.get_service('ConversionUploadService')
            for conversion in conversion_data:
                upload_conversion = conversion_upload_service_pb2.UploadCallConversionRequest()
                upload_conversion.conversion_action = conversion_action_resource_name
                upload_conversion.conversion_value = conversion['conversion_value']
                upload_conversion.call_duration_seconds = 120  # Example call duration
                if 'gclid' in conversion:
                    upload_conversion.gclid = conversion['gclid']
                elif 'gbraid' in conversion:
                    upload_conversion.order_id = conversion['gbraid']
                elif 'wbraid' in conversion:
                    upload_conversion.order_id = conversion['wbraid']
                response = conversion_upload_service.upload_call_conversions(
                    customer_id=self.client.customer_id,
                    requests=[upload_conversion]
                )
                print(f"Uploaded conversion for {upload_conversion.gclid or upload_conversion.order_id} successfully.")
        except GoogleAdsException as ex:
            print(f'Request with ID "{ex.request_id}" failed with status "{ex.error.code().name}" and includes the following errors:')
            for error in ex.failure.errors:
                print(f'\tError with message "{error.message}".')
        except Exception as e:
            print(f"An error occurred while uploading conversions: {e}")
```

# LangChain

Building applications with LLMs through composability

Looking for the JS/TS version? Check out LangChain.js.

**Production Support:** As you move your LangChains into production, we'd love to offer more comprehensive support.

Please fill out this form and we'll set up a dedicated support Slack channel.

## Quick Install

`pip install langchain`

or

`conda install langchain -c conda-forge`

## 🤔 What is this?

Large language models (LLMs) are emerging as a transformative technology, enabling developers to build applications that they previously could not. However, using these LLMs in isolation is often insufficient for creating a truly powerful app - the real power comes when you can combine them with other sources of computation or knowledge.

This library aims to assist in the development of those types of applications. Common examples of these applications include:

**❓ Question Answering over specific documents**

- Documentation

- End-to-end Example: Question Answering over Notion Database

**🤖 Agents**

- Documentation

- End-to-end Example: GPT+WolframAlpha

## 📖 Documentation

Please see [here](https://python.langchain.com) for full documentation on:

- Getting started (installation, setting up the environment, simple examples)

- How-To examples (demos, integrations, helper functions)

- Reference (full API docs)

- Resources (high-level explanation of core concepts)

# Google Ads Converter App

The Google Ads Converter App is a Python application designed to facilitate the uploading of offline conversion data to Google Ads using the Google Ads API. This application reads conversion data from a local CSV file and uploads it to a specified Google Ads Conversion Action using appropriate identifiers (GCLID, GBRAID, or WBRAID). It also implements OAuth2 authentication and includes basic error handling and logging.

## Main Functions

- **Read CSV File**: Reads offline conversion data from a specified CSV file.
- **Authenticate with Google Ads API**: Implements OAuth2 authentication to securely connect to the Google Ads API.
- **Upload Conversions**: Uploads conversion data to a specified Google Ads Conversion Action.
- **Error Handling**: Provides basic error handling for file reading and API requests.

## Installation

To run the Google Ads Converter App, you need to install the required dependencies. Follow the steps below to set up your environment:

1. **Install Python**: Ensure you have Python 3.6 or higher installed on your machine. You can download it from [python.org](https://www.python.org/downloads/).

2. **Install Required Libraries**: Use `pip` to install the necessary libraries. Open your terminal or command prompt and run the following command:

   ```bash
   pip install google-ads
   ```

3. **Set Up Google Ads API Credentials**: You will need to create a Google Cloud project and enable the Google Ads API. Obtain your `client_id`, `client_secret`, `developer_token`, and `refresh_token`. Store these credentials securely.

4. **Prepare Your CSV File**: Create a CSV file containing your offline conversion data. The file should have the following format:

   ```
   gclid,gbraid,wbraid,conversion_value
   ```

   Ensure that each row contains the appropriate identifiers and conversion value.

## How to Use the Application

1. **Modify the Code**: Open the `main.py` file and replace the placeholders for `client_id`, `client_secret`, `developer_token`, and `refresh_token` with your actual credentials. Also, update the `file_path` variable with the path to your CSV file.

   ```python
   self.api_handler = GoogleAdsAPIHandler(client_id='your_client_id', client_secret='your_client_secret', developer_token='your_developer_token', refresh_token='your_refresh_token')
   file_path = 'path_to_your_csv_file.csv'
   ```

2. **Run the Application**: Execute the `main.py` file to start the application. You can do this by running the following command in your terminal:

   ```bash
   python main.py
   ```

3. **Upload Conversions**: Click the "Upload Conversions" button in the GUI to read the CSV file and upload the conversions to Google Ads. You will see success or error messages in the console.

## Error Handling

The application includes basic error handling for common issues such as file not found errors and API request failures. If an error occurs, it will be printed to the console for your review.

## Conclusion

The Google Ads Converter App simplifies the process of uploading offline conversion data to Google Ads. By following the installation and usage instructions, you can quickly set up and run the application to manage your conversion data effectively.

For further assistance or support, please refer to the [Google Ads API documentation](https://developers.google.com/google-ads/api/docs/start) for more detailed information.
```
